As you know, `The Weekly Challenge`, primarily focus on **Perl** and **Raku**. During the **Week #018**, we received solutions to **["The Weekly Challenge - 018"](/blog/perl-weekly-challenge-018)** by `Orestis Zekai` in **Python**. It was pleasant surprise to receive solutions in something other than **Perl** and **Raku**. Ever since regular team members also started contributing in other languages like **Ada**, **APL**, **Awk**, **Basic**, **Bash**, **Bc**, **Befunge**, **Bourne Shell**, **BQN**, **Brainfuck**, **C3**, **C**, **CESIL**, **Chef**, **COBOL**, **Coconut**, **C Shell**, **C++**, **Clojure**, **Crystal**, **D**, **Dart**, **Elm**, **Erlang**, **Excel VBA**, **Fish**, **Forth**, **Fortran**, **Gembase**, **GNAT**, **Go**, **Haskell**, **Haxe**, **HTML**, **Idris**, **IO**, **J**, **Janet**, **Java**, **JavaScript**, **Julia**, **Kotlin**, **Lisp**, **Logo**, **Lua**, **M4**, **Macro Processor**, **Miranda**, **MMIX**, **Mumps**, **Myrddin**, **Nim**, **Nix**, **Node.js**, **Nuweb**, **OCaml**, **Odin**, **Ook**, **Pascal**, **PHP**, **Python**, **PostgreSQL**, **Postscript**, **Prolog**, **R**, **Rexx**, **Ring**, **Ruby**, **Rust**, **Scala**, **Scheme**, **Sed**, **Smalltalk**, **SQL**, **SVG**, **Swift**, **Tcl**, **Visual Basic**, **Wolfram**, **XSLT** and **Zig**.

Please find below guest contributions.
